 isamen Google Assistant diya gaya he or isamen inbilt spikar diya gaya he
 In India, Google has started launching its smart speakers from early 2018
 Google Nest Hub bharat main chock or charcol color verient main uplabdh he
 It can be purchased from Flipkart, Reliance Digital, Croma and Tata Click
 haal hi main google ne elaan kiya he ki ab Google Assistant hindi bhi samajhegaa or aap isse hindi main interact bhi kar sakate hai

 yani inamen bydaree nahin hoti or na hi aap sim laga sakate hai
 How to setup Google Nest Hub It is easy to setup
 box se Google Nest Hub nikaal kar die gaye cabel ko socket main or nest hub divaais se plag karen
 You will get the option to connect as soon as the device is turned on
 apane smartphone par Google Home ap downlod karen

 Here your Nest device will show and you have to connect to it
 jis wifai router se aapkaa phone conect he use se Google Nest Hub bhi conect hoga
 Design and Build Quality The Google Nest Hub is compact, handy and easy to carry anywhere
 haalanki isamen bydaree nahin he
 The build quality is good and it looks beautiful
 study teble, bedside teble yaa phir aapaki marji ‚Äì aap ise kahin bhi rakh sakate hai

 isamen camera nahin he

 Google Nest Hub ke back panel par ek switch he
 This allows the microphone to be muted
 iske saath hi wolum control karne ke liye batan bhi die gaye hai
 Display The Google Nest Hub has a 7-inch screen with a resolution of 1,024X600
 tach screen panel he or yahaan koi batan nahin he
 You either control it from the app or touch and use it
 disple brit he or iskaa britaness edjust kar sakate hai
 The job of ambient sensors is that if you turn off your room light, then the display of Google Nest Hub gets dimmed
 disple par timming bhi dikhti rahegi, lekin ye ankhon ko nahin chubhta he
 Bezels have been given around the display and no front camera has been provided, which is a good thing about privacy
 parforsmens, software or khaasiyatye aapke ghar main persolas acystant kii tarah kaam karegaa
 You can give commands to it from anywhere in the whole room
 isamen powerful microphone hai
 However, if your room is too big then you may have problems

 Hey, you can ask any question to this by giving a Google command
 isamen diya gaya spikar zyada powerful nahin he
 But it is okay for basic use

 yah faisla hoicourt ne us janhit yachika ke tahat diya tha, jisamen whatsap kii shering policy par sawaal uthaaya gaya he

 iskaa makasad yuzars tak sateek vigyaapan pahunchaana tha

 use jeevanabhar ksht rahata he

 bhado ke ravivaar main ye kaam karne se bachein--ravivaar ke din suryaast se purv namak kaa upyog na karen

 -yah bhi kaha jaataa he ki ravivaar ko raat hone se pehle sambhog nahin karnaa chahie

 -aamtaur par log ravivaar ko hi bal kataate hai

 isliye isadin bal kataane se or sir main tel maalish or doodh ko jalaane kaa kaary nahin karnaa chahie

 -is din nile, kaale va grey rang ke vastra na pahanen

 " clinest railway stationvijeta: jodhpurjit kii vajah: 2016 main ise swatchta main bharat ke railway steshnon main 187waan sthaan hasil hua tha, or aaj isane bharat ke sabase svachh railway stesan kaa darja hasil kar liya haiyah stesan 2016 ke ek survey ke anusaar, railway steshnon main 187wein sthaan par tha

 ab isane bharat ke sabase saaf railway stesan ke liye india today safigiri aword jeeta he

 a massive fire broke out after the accident that occurred near Hyderabad city late on Saturday, as the tanker was carrying 40 thousand liters of fuel
 reporton se pataa chalata he ki tel tanker kaa driver tanker ko sadak kinare khadaa karke andar so gaya tha

 bas main bacchon or mahilaon samet kareeb 50 log savaar the
 Regional police officer Muhammad Farooq gave this information at the scene
 faruk ne taaya, bas kaa chaalak niyantran kho baitha or usne tel tanker ko peeche se takkar maar di

 unhone bataaya ki marane waalon main bachche or mahilaayein shaamil hai

 bharat or pakistan mul ke ye khilaadi is team main shandaar pradarshan bhi kar rahe hai
 This team is none other than Oman's team
 oman ne shandaar pradarshan karte hue buudhvaar ko ireland ko bhi haraaya he
 It is the same Ireland that has defeated Pakistan and West Indies in the World Cup
 sirf itnaa hi nahin oman team ke koching staff main bhi zyada se zyada bharat or srilankai mul ke log hai
 The five players of Indian origin who have confirmed their place in this team are Munish Ansari, Ajay Lalcheta, Jatinder Singh, Rajesh Kumar and Vaibhav Wategavkar
 munish ansaari kaa janm indore main hua he or unki tarif rahul dravid or wasim akram bhi kar chuke hai

 laalcheta saurashtra ke liye bhi khel chuke hai
 He has got a place in Saurashtra's Under 16, Under 19 and Under 22 teams
 sirf laalcheta hi nahin rajesh kumaar kaa janm bhi gujarat ke paalan main hua he

 He is a good batsman in Oman's team
 abhi tak oman team ke liye 10 tii20 match khelte hue kareeb 18 kii ausat se 175 ran bana chuke hai

 oman ke spin bowling coach sunil joshi hai
 Sunil Joshi has played 15 Tests and 69 odis for India
 1999 main sunil joshi ne south africa ke khilaaf shandaar gendbaaji karte hue sirf 6 ran dekar paanch wicket liye the

 vijay bharadwaj oman team ke fielding coach hai
 Bhardwaj has played one-day matches for India
 bharadwaj ne apni pehali siries main shandaar ol rounding pradarshan karte hue "main of da siries" award jeeta tha
 Bhardwaj has also been the coach of Karnataka Ranji Trophy
 tippaniyan Players of Pakistan origin are in this team, Sultan Ahmed who is captain, Khawar Ali, Zeeshan Siddiqui, Bilal Khan, Adnan Illayas and Aamir Ali

 team ho to aisi
